msg:The room is big and clean. The sanitation is very good, but the service is really bad.
First of all, there is no security guard to guide the parking space when driving into the hotel, and you have to find it by yourself; there is no doorman service when entering and exiting the hotel. There is indeed a reception desk next to the revolving door of the hotel, but every time I go in and out, I see two doormen or experienced people chatting and laughing behind the reception desk, and they don‚Äôt even ask guests how they are when they come in; the funniest part is here: I ordered takeout in the room, and the first time it was delivered by a robot. After 20 minutes, I ordered another one, but it was not delivered for a long time. I wanted to call the front desk, but the room landline could not get through to the front desk at all, so I had to run down to get it myself. I ran to ask the front desk first, and the girl at the front desk immediately answered me: the delivery robot is broken. I said that it was just delivered to me 20 minutes ago, how could it be broken. Then a man who looked like a manager told me that the takeout was in the takeout box at the door. I asked why it was not delivered by a robot? The manager answered that the takeout guy had to tell them, and they would deliver it. I think if the two people standing at the reception desk have nothing to do, they can often check whether there is any takeaway that has not been delivered upstairs. The service attitude of the hotel is really disappointing. However, some service staff I saw in the guest room area were very good and greeted us proactively, which made me feel warm. The main problem is that the service at the front desk and lobby is not in place. I hope the hotel management can see some improvements.

Fruits, cookies, and three kinds of carbonated drinks are welcome.
The room also provides paid disposable bath towels and bathtub covers.
The children had a beautiful bath, and there was no need to worry about cross infection.
The only drawback was that when we checked in at around 5 pm, the front desk said that the cleaning was not finished yet, so we put our luggage first and they urged us to urge the cleaning progress. But later we learned that the cleaning was completed, but the supervisor had not checked and confirmed it yet.

Overall satisfied, there was a phone call after check-out, and the deposit deduction was also confirmed by phone.

msg:I took my kids to Lanxi during the Qingming Festival. The hotel is located in the city center, with convenient parking and transportation. The front desk upgraded the executive room for free. The highest floors have an unbeatable view. Outside the window is the three rivers of Lanxi. This should be the most luxurious hotel in Lanxi, but the price is at the level of a business hotel in a second-tier city.

The decoration is very new, and the facilities are also luxurious. The small refrigerator, safe, and bathtub are five-star standard. Hansgrohe and Duravit bathrooms, welcome fruit plates, drinks and snacks are also good, and 4 bottles of water are placed at a time. The children also like to soak in the bathtub. Originally, they only booked one night, but decided to stay another night that night.

If you must find some shortcomings, the pillow is a bit collapsed, and the sleep is not very comfortable. I hope it can be improved. In addition, the breakfast for 9-year-old children is half price, which is a bit unpleasant. Overall, it is still great. If I come to Lanxi to play next time, I will definitely choose this one again.
